  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3186a73c-c47d-470c-9533-252df36d2326'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer417831328" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3238187189424130122"><b>
  <u>
    <i>SERIOUSLY??!!</i>
  </u>
</b> I am so freakin' angry hurt disappointed annoyed irritated upset, name it and I'm that with this book. <b>
  <u>
    <i>This book, quite frankly was horrible.</i>
  </u>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391746ra/754312.gif' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>
  <u>
    <i>The 3 Stars I'm giving this book are ONLY FOR ALL THE GUY CHARACTERS, especially COLE.</i>
  </u>
</b> and also for how the POVs were written. It was brilliant hot one pov lead to the other. AMAZING<br/><br/>I mean after such brilliant first two books of the series; Reason to Breathe and Barely Breathing, we get such a shitty third </span>
  <span id="freeText3238187189424130122" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>
    <i>SERIOUSLY??!!</i>
  </u>
</b> I am so freakin' angry hurt disappointed annoyed irritated upset, name it and I'm that with this book. <b>
  <u>
    <i>This book, quite frankly was horrible.</i>
  </u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391746ra/754312.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <u>
    <i>The 3 Stars I'm giving this book are ONLY FOR ALL THE GUY CHARACTERS, especially COLE.</i>
  </u>
</b> and also for how the POVs were written. It was brilliant hot one pov lead to the other. AMAZING<br><br>I mean after such brilliant first two books of the series; Reason to Breathe and Barely Breathing, we get such a shitty third novel: Out of Breath. Its pretty darn disappointing because you just bloody expect A LOT after RoB and BB and after waiting since months. :|<br><br>THIS BOOK HAD NOTHING. It was dragged and stuck at the same time. The story wasn't moving. It had no plot. Wtv they were 'keeping' from each other was so fucking stupid I wanted to hit someone.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391746ra/754313.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I am just to angry and irritated at the moment because this book was so bad.<br><br><b>
  <i>AND OMFG, what the hell was with the ending? I was like 'are you fucking kidding me?!' One of the worst endings I've read. I hope we freakin' get a novella or something after that shitty ending.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391746i/754314.gif" width="300" height="215" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><u>
  <i>YOU GUYS HAVE NO IDEA HOW BADLY ITS HURTING ME TO WRITE AND POST THIS REVIEW. </i>

<div id="review_502364596" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/502364596" />
    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/502364596?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer502364596" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3770455751980468029">3.5 stars!<br/><br/>I am devastatingly disappointed with this book since I had such high expectations, the first two books ‘Reason to Breathe' and ‘Barely Breathing’ were brilliantly written and both of them left us with huge cliffy’s and what makes this even worse is that we had to wait such a long time for this book to be released.<br/> <br/>Normally I would agree that Rebecca Donovan is an exceptional writer who basically holds all your emotions in the palm of her hands while you are reading her books. Perhaps, </span>
  <span id="freeText3770455751980468029" style="display:none">3.5 stars!<br><br>I am devastatingly disappointed with this book since I had such high expectations, the first two books ‘Reason to Breathe' and ‘Barely Breathing’ were brilliantly written and both of them left us with huge cliffy’s and what makes this even worse is that we had to wait such a long time for this book to be released.<br> <br>Normally I would agree that Rebecca Donovan is an exceptional writer who basically holds all your emotions in the palm of her hands while you are reading her books. Perhaps, too much expectation went into this book because of the high standard we are accustomed to from her. No doubt, this series is very emotional, somewhat disturbing and very upsetting to think they some people have this in their lives.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787310.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I was infested with blackness, scorching and marring my insides, feeding on the guilt and hate that had taken root so long ago. It intertwined with every cell, and there was no hiding from it any longer. I couldn’t feel. I couldn’t think. I couldn’t move without triggering an unfathomable pain that would leave me begging to end the suffering, just as my mother intended."</b><br><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787311.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyone reading this book, a little advice…..<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787312.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Getting down to the story…<br>So Emma left Evan and went off to college at the end of book two with not even a Goodbye or anything…<br> <br><b>
  <i> “I love him more than he will ever know. And because of that, I choose his happiness.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>Two years later Emma is still struggling with her broken heart, the voices in her head and is struggling just to survive…<br>Emma isn’t living, she is just <i>Breathing</i>, an empty shell of the girl she used to be.<br><br><b>"She’s just been … existing since she left Weslyn. There’s no … light in her eyes. No purpose. No drive."</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787313.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With the help of her roommates, Emma is forced into doing things and trying to bring some excitement into her life.<br> <br>This is when Emma meets Cole. I have nothing but love for this boy and I truly feel sorry for him because of what Emma did to him emotionally.<br>HURTING someone no matter what the circumstances are <b>IS NOT COOL EMMA!!</b><br> <br>Yes, Cole was a ‘filler’ but he accepted the fact that Emma had been through something, he never pushed, he cared and at the end of the day he accepted any bullshit that Emma did or said because he just wanted her…. It was just sex, nothing more to Emma. They were not dating even though they spent so much time together.<br><br><b>"I gripped the tense muscles along his back as he moved into me, exploring me deeper. The charge intensified, possessing my senses. It became all that I could feel, all that I needed, as it streamed through every inch of my body. The emptiness was swept away, and I would give anything not to be devoured by it again."</b><br> <br>When Emma gets the call that her mother killed herself she is forced to go to her home town that she ran away from, which eventually leads to breaking her down even more. Memories of what happened eat at Emma alive and she wants to numb the pain… with alcohol?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404559i/787314.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So Emma never drank and now shes always drunk? She hated her mother and her drinking and now is doing EXACTLY what she did?<br><b>
  <u>I REALLY DON’T GET HOW THIS EVEN MAKES ANY SENSE??</u>
</b><br>Who is this IMPOSTER and what have they done with the EMMA we knew???<br> <br>Sara, bless this girls soul, she is amazing and I would love to have a friend like her by my side.<br>She takes care of Emma until Emma is so out of it but there is only one person that will save her, that always saves her Evan…<br> <br><b>
  <i> “Every breath I breathe is because of you. Even when your weren't there to save me, you were my reason to breathe. And for that I will always love you. Always</i>
</b><br> <br>I love Evan, I’ve loved him from the first time I met him and I have great respect for this boy. For someone to still be this way after he was hurt , wronged and also broken is astounding.<br> <br>He comes back to California for the summer where Emma and Cole are and YES, this is such a big FCUK UP! Emma’s actions here cannot and I will not allow her to blame this on her broken past and fcuked up family! This is ALL EMMA!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787315.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Evan and Emma have been through so much in their journey together and as much as Emma wants Evan to hate her for what she did to him, he cant..<br><br><b>"Evan Mathews, you can tell yourself and everyone else that you’re here to get answers, for closure. But the truth is, you love her. You have always loved her. You will always love her. You’re here because you can’t walk away. You saw how broken and empty she was back in Weslyn, and you had to follow her. You’ll never be able to let her go. You’re here because … it’s where you belong, with her.’"</b><br> <br>Emma was frustrating at times, so much that I wanted to scream at her or shake her out of it.<br>I do understand what she’s been to and that she’s DROWNING in her hurt and pain and is STRUGGLING to see the LIGHT, to Find her Breath…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787316.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787317.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Breathe, Emma. Take a deep breath.’"<br><br>"Let it all out, Emma. Find your way back to us.’"</b><br> <br>I know and understand Emma has been dealt a shitty hand in life but she was really extreme. The <b>running</b> and depressions and crying was a bit much and really dragged out. So many emotions which ended up being repetitions to fill the pages just left us irritated.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787318.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On the one hand Emma is running and running and not eating etc, the picture in my head was that she was lifeless looking and anorexic?<br>The next thing people are talking about how stunning Emma looks and her great legs? It just didn’t make sense.<br><br><b>"I’m afraid to kiss you,’ he confessed, his words floating through the air in the hush. ‘I’m afraid that if I kiss you, I won’t want to stop. I can feel you tense every time we touch, and I don’t want to do anything that will make you walk away from me."</b><br> <br>To me it seemed that EVERYONE in this book was constantly babying Emma <b> ALL. THE. TIME</b> It was exhausting!!!!<br>Yet another girl that could do literally ANY shit but everyone still forgave her and loved her?<br>The overall plot felt a bit empty to me. I wish I could edit this book and take out all the shit which actually did not need to be there. I think that would have made this a 5star read because it really has 5 star potential!<br>Rebecca definitely should have listened to the ‘Less is More’ concept!<br> <br><br>In order for Emma and Evan to get anywhere is for them both to let each other 'in'....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404559i/787319.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The writing was utterly confusing with the different POV’s and Evan’s side in italics but then Emma had a thought and it was also in Italic?<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404559i/787320.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> “I couldn't catch my breath. I buried my face in his shirt. He was my reason for existing. It was his words that pulled me to the surface. His breath that saved me. And now, his arms that held me within this life, unable to give up. He was my strength, and the love I didn't have for myself. And I couldn't live without him more than he could let me go.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404559ra/787321.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>During one conversation the writing is switched to different POV’s which really doesn’t make sense and im like? WHAAAAAT? Ohhhh… this is Evan talking etc.<br>This was completely stupid and unnecessary and not WELL done!<br> <br>I finished this book because I felt like I owed it to MYSELF for the time invested in this series, however I am utterly PISSED off right now!!<br>So we get PAGES AND PAGES of ‘FILLERS’ but Rebecca could not write a decent Epilogue?<br>The story felt <b>Unfinished</b><br>I literally blinked, literally and it was over????!!!!<br> <br><b>
  <i>"I just had to remember, there was always a choice. And I chose to live. I chose to love. I chose to breathe."</i>
</b><br> <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><b> “I don't understand. You still...love me?"<br>"Yeah, I do. And I know you're not the same girl. But I'm in love with you, Emma. I fell in love with you all over again this summer. People change. I know this. And we'll continue to change. That just means I'll get to fall in love with you again. Because no matter what happens in our lives, what I feel for you will survive anything.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404559i/787322.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Look, no matter what I thought about this book, I’m REALLY REALLY glad that Emma and Evan have found their way back to each other because God knows they both deserve it!!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/371111504?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Doreen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Doreen" href="/user/show/6905976-doreen">Doreen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer371111504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14531189191947221319">You just know that I will be the one sitting at the computer screen repeatedly clicking refresh in the hopes that there will at least be like a book summary or something. I will not for a second waver. I will sit here religiously and click refresh because this is how much I am addicted to this series. I realize that this is not healthy and I seriously do not give a damn. I am and will forever be addicted to Emma and Evan. When the release date is posted I will bite my fingernails in anticipation</span>
  <span id="freeText14531189191947221319" style="display:none">You just know that I will be the one sitting at the computer screen repeatedly clicking refresh in the hopes that there will at least be like a book summary or something. I will not for a second waver. I will sit here religiously and click refresh because this is how much I am addicted to this series. I realize that this is not healthy and I seriously do not give a damn. I am and will forever be addicted to Emma and Evan. When the release date is posted I will bite my fingernails in anticipation. A day before the release I will stay up, read the first two books and on the last page of the second book I will immediately leave my house, got to the nearest book store, and stay there until I finish the third book. Then the day after the third book comes out, I will read all the books in order. I will then be satisfied because the book will have ended the way that I want. With Emma and Evan HAPPY! If anyone deserves happiness then it's them. Okay. Now post a release date already because my fingers are starting to tire from pressing refresh and people probably think I'm a little weird. Too bad I don't care. POST THE DAMN DATE!!!!! AND SUMMARY!!!!!!!<br /><br />Thank the good lord that I have characters left because this is going to be a whole new level of difficult. Most of you on this page right now. Reading this review have been with Emma and Evan since the beginning. I have held on to Emma and Evan for dear life. They are pretty much at the top of my list of favourite characters. The first book was captivated because Emma's story is one that breaks the heart into a million pieces. I'm book two Emma's heart shatters even more though you don't expect that it could. In book three, Emma attempts to rebuild her heart all on her own but she just can't.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ She never could built it back on her own. She needed Evan. She has always needed Evan. I've never hurt so much for a character than I did for Emma. Talk about the world being against you. She was the evidence. She made it though. She made it out of her tunnel and at the end she found Evan waiting with open arms. They both definitely had things to work out but it came together. It wasn't a forced happily ever after. They didn't fake anything. They just lived their lives each day with love. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_626427072" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/626427072" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/626427072?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews?shelf=july-2013">july-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer626427072" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18074597492298600012"><b>4.5~stars<br/><br/>There are moments in life you'll never forget. Moments that brand your heart. Moments that shatter your soul. Moments that are infinite. <br/><br/>New emotions are created in these moments.<br/><br/>Time stops in these moments.<br/><br/>We <i>lose</i> ourselves in these moments...</b><br/><br/>We all shared this moment at the end of <i>Reason to Breathe</i> Our happily ever after was ripped away only to be replaced by emotions we didn't even know existed. Emotions created by a moment that caused us to stop breathing. A fearless ending that sho</span>
  <span id="freeText18074597492298600012" style="display:none"><b>4.5~stars<br /><br />There are moments in life you'll never forget. Moments that brand your heart. Moments that shatter your soul. Moments that are infinite. <br /><br />New emotions are created in these moments.<br /><br />Time stops in these moments.<br /><br />We <i>lose</i> ourselves in these moments...</b><br /><br />We all shared this moment at the end of <i>Reason to Breathe</i> Our happily ever after was ripped away only to be replaced by emotions we didn't even know existed. Emotions created by a moment that caused us to stop breathing. A fearless ending that shocked the world. <br /><br />After that, we grieved. <br /><br />We grieved for the unknown.<br /><br />That grief however, was replaced by anger. <br /><br />After being physically assaulted by emotions and a cliffhanger heard round the world, Rebecca Donovan turned right around and emotionally raped us with <i>Barely Breathing</i>. However, we insanely and greedily kept coming back for more (I also wanted to judo chop her right in the f---fagina....repeatedly).<br /><br />Regardless, we just wanted more! In <i>Out Of Breath</i>, Rebecca Donovan gives us more. <br /><br />At first, I was selfishly disappointed. I wanted instant resolution. I wanted to open the book and fall right into Emma and Evan. It's been so long, too long. I didn't <i>want</i> to know the new characters. I didn't <i>want</i> to know Cole. This is Emma and Evan's story dammit! Give me what I want!!<br /><br />Rebecca Donovan changed what I wanted!<br /><br />Without me even being aware of it, she gave me something I didn't even <i>know</i> I wanted. Instead of constantly looking ahead for my resolution. She made it okay for me to be in the present. I stopped looking for something else and found something new, being able to focus on the now. Enjoying the now. Enjoying Cole. Give yourself some time, you'll get there. You'll be completely happy in the present, and realize that this detour is just part of the journey. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I listen to silence. And you...you have a lot to say."</i>
</b><br /><br />I knew it was only matter of time before Evan and Emma's worlds collided again and once it did, I was lost. Lost in a way that you know exactly where you are, but searching to find that place, <i>the</i> place. Resolution. Closure. <br /><br />What I found so amazingly powerful, was the alternating POVs. It was done in such a unique way, I was surprise by its fluency. It was unique and flawless. We experience the same moment in alternating POVs, at the same time!!! WAIT...what!?? Yes, the chapters weren't split into alternating POVs, but the story happened while instantaneously allowing the reader to see the moment from both Emma and Evan's eyes. You'd think that would cause some serious reader whiplash, but Rebecca Donovan's writing talent knows no limits. Emma and Evan have the exact same moment at the exact same time (okay maybe not <i>exactly</i> at the same time, that would just be cray cray, but you get the picture). This unique element brought the story alive.<br /><br />I was hoping for a little more out of the epilogue, but maybe I'm just being greedy. Maybe I just wasn't ready to let go. Maybe I just wanted more. None of which are bad things. Either way, I was hoping to see just a little bit more of <i>their</i> future. <br /><br />Rebecca Donovan tore my world apart two years ago, but the best part was letting her put it back together again, and in this moment...I am whole.<br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br />More reviews a at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18074597492298600012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_414682834" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/414682834" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/414682834?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer414682834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12338605397432258739"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380334158ra/693623.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And the winner of the biggest book disappointment of the year goes to.....<br/><br/>Out of Breath by Rebecca Donovan!!!<br/><br/>And to think this was probably my most anticipated book release of 2013!!<br/><br/>Yeah....instead, here I am! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391261ra/753461.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I feel like this book also suffered from the "series syndrome"! The author made us wait a year for the final installment in the series. And let's face it....the more time that goes by, the less and less I am going to care. So as an author you better <b>BRING IT</b>! Not to mention I don't necessa</span>
  <span id="freeText12338605397432258739" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380334158ra/693623.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the winner of the biggest book disappointment of the year goes to.....<br><br>Out of Breath by Rebecca Donovan!!!<br><br>And to think this was probably my most anticipated book release of 2013!!<br><br>Yeah....instead, here I am! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391261ra/753461.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I feel like this book also suffered from the "series syndrome"! The author made us wait a year for the final installment in the series. And let's face it....the more time that goes by, the less and less I am going to care. So as an author you better <b>BRING IT</b>! Not to mention I don't necessarily want to have to go back and re-read the other books in the series. But after a year and 200+ books later the odds that I am going to remember anything are going to be slim to none. <br><br>So...on to the book itself. It really seemed like I was reading two different books. The part before Evan "comes back". Where were meet the new and improved Emma. The Emma almost two years after <b>SHE</b> left Evan!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391261ra/753462.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Listen Emma...cut the shit!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391261ra/753463.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All the drinking--it's NOT ATTRACTIVE. Pull it together! You're not doing a very good job of making me like you. At. All. <br><br>Which brings us to the part after Evan "comes back". This was really just a bunch of filler. No plot. Nothing happened.....maybe a little running here, a swim in the ocean there, a conversation here, a <s>little</s>, okay a <b>LOT</b> of blushing there! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391261i/753464.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Who am I kidding, I was bored before too. At this point...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391261ra/753465.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now I just need to rant about a few things....<br><br>1) Coincidences....and the fact that there were <b>WAY</b> too many!<br> --What are the odds that Evan's BFFs live 3 houses down from Cole and <br> that Emma will just "happen" to go to a party there? And all of <br> his friends recognized her?? <br> --What are the odds that people that know Jonathan will be camping <br> right next to Emma and she'll hear them talking about him?<br> --Evan and Cole knew each other???<br><b>NOT GOOD. SLIM TO NONE. NOT LIKELY. ARE YOU KIDDING ME?</b><br><br>2) Cole....poor sweet, innocent Cole. Emma fucked you over. And honestly I am really not sure what purpose you served in this twisted story. Plus your character was TOO similar to Evan's. <br><br>3) Emma and her gold-plated pussy. Once again we have another heroine that <b>EVERY</b> guy is in love with.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391261ra/753466.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4) The whole drinking thing. This just didn't make sense. She didn't drink at all the first year and half after she left Evan but now she's constantly drunk?!?!?! And why are all of her friends acting like it's their fault that Emma's drinking?!?! <br><br>4a) And speaking of the friends....I honestly didn't find any of them very likable but all they did was coddle Emma. Like she was this fragile, suicidal girl that had to be babysat 24 hours a day. <br><br>5) The use of the word jeering. Does anyone use this word in every day conversations?? Emma sure seemed to "jeer" a lot. BTW--I had to look up what the hell jeering was. <br><br>6) Why was everyone so mad at Evan?? All of her friends (with the exception of Serena) were mean to Evan....yet, Evan's friends were nice and welcoming to Emma?!?! And I repeat....SHE'S. THE. ONE. THAT. LEFT. HIM.<br><br>7) The alternating POVs. While, yes, alternating POVs are nice....just not in the <b>SAME</b> conversation. It was confusing...the use of the italics to change POVs--mid thought. Especially when there were times she italicized (is that even a word - lol) the wrong conversation. <br><br>And that brings us to the <b>EPILOGUE</b>...or the lack there of. After all that we were put through during Reason to Breathe and Barely Breathing all we got was some shit about <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the cousins <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>??? That's it?!?! I mean WTF Rebecca?? WTF?? We deserved SO MUCH MORE! Biggest. Disappointment. Ever.<br><br>The End.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391261ra/753467.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_331358005" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/331358005" />
    <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites"><img alt="Alexis *Reality Bites*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1404308282p2/5587514.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/331358005?book_show_action=true">May 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=awaiting-release">awaiting-release</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer331358005" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5605942154540619659">Minor Spoilers- mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>3 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: New Adult Romance<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378019i/733401.png' alt=' photo 6688f920-1_zps9bd95e03.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378019ra/733402.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mekalijO1o1rccyxzo1_500_zps2111fd60.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I don’t even know what to write. I have a love hate relationship with this book. I love Evan, Cole and Jared. I disliked Emma and hated her actions. It was rare that she was in a scene and I enjoyed reading it enough to be content. Nope, her character kept me in an emotionally edgy state at all times. In fact I spent most of the book like this<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378019ra/733403.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_m2ognmflj41r9dtlj_zps01590c65.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>Utterly. <br/><br/>Frustrated. </b><br/><br/>Now don’t get me wrong I don’t min</span>
  <span id="freeText5605942154540619659" style="display:none">Minor Spoilers- mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>3 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378019i/733401.png" alt=" photo 6688f920-1_zps9bd95e03.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378019ra/733402.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mekalijO1o1rccyxzo1_500_zps2111fd60.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I don’t even know what to write. I have a love hate relationship with this book. I love Evan, Cole and Jared. I disliked Emma and hated her actions. It was rare that she was in a scene and I enjoyed reading it enough to be content. Nope, her character kept me in an emotionally edgy state at all times. In fact I spent most of the book like this<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378019ra/733403.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m2ognmflj41r9dtlj_zps01590c65.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Utterly. <br><br>Frustrated. </b><br><br>Now don’t get me wrong I don’t mind being pissed off by a character.. However, to be in a consistent<b> somebody-please-put-ME-in-a-padded-cell</b> state of mind due to her actions…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378019ra/733404.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m95pkl0xy31rvz69h_zpsebbde87e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not cool…<br><br>Unfortunately compared to books 1 and 2 in this series Out of Breath just fell short.<br> <b>For me.<br><br> Personally. </b><br><br>It just.. It just completely failed to captivate me or move me in the same way its predecessors did. But hey, that’s my opinion. One I rested and actually thought on before rating and typing this review up to post. <br><br>At the end of Barely Breathing Emma makes the decision to leave Evan behind by taking off across the country to attend Stanford alone. Book 3, Out of Breath picks up two years later with Emma still struggling to move on from her choice… Sadly Emma is pretty much a shell of her former self. She is alive going day to day without truly living. She is still in close contact with her best friend Sara. And she also has roommates who by the way help boost some scenes with their wit and colorful personalities. <br><br>Tragedy strikes and Emma and Evan cross paths. What Evan finds is not the girl he once knew. <br><br><i>
  <b>'She was still breathtakingly beautiful. Except for the vacancy in her eyes.'</b>
</i> ~Evan<br><br>If you thought reading through the abuse Emma suffered was bad..Well reading while she lives in this..this constant state of depression was just as bad.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378019ra/733405.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mkyxmw0Ex31rfxftro1_r1_500_zpsd7bb19bb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both Sara and Evan fight to free Emma from the firm grip she holds on to death and quite frankly it is very sad.<br><br>Out of Breath will leave some fans mad, others sadly disappointed, few satisfied and most just a plain old wreck. Like me.*points thumb at chest*<br> <br>On a side note: Readers do get a bonus in Out of Breath; Evan's pov which I thought was nice.<br><br><b>
  <u>My Casting</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380365019i/716843.jpg" alt=" photo 23858c71-05cc-4989-ab62-1ee6d32b6d02_zps52b38177.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br><b>-First</b> things first though, I need to know if Cole will be getting his own book, seriously I fell hard for his character and I would love to see him happy. Yes, happy in a nice stand alone book with over 300 pages of romance. Just though I would throw that out in to the universe!<br><br><b>-Second,</b> I knew it… I freaking knew it in my gut that Emma and Evan would spend a good deal of the book separated. What shocked me was Emma’s recklessness at life, with her life and about life in general. Shit does that even make sense what I just said? Whatever, like I said this book wrecked me.<br><br><b>-Third,</b> I did not need 300+ pages of sad, depressingly drunk and might I add suicidal Emma. They really should stuck her ass in rehab for alcoholism and depression. Not sure how partying the summer away was suppose to help her out. No. Rehab, that chick was in need of some serious therapy and self meditation or whatever the hell it is they do in rehab.<br><br><b>-Fourth,</b> the epilogue. Are you effing kidding me? That’s all we get?<b> WHAT. THE. FRICK.</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Overall</u>
</b> I decided to go with 3 stars because I felt caught in the middle on how to rate it. And even though I loved Cole’s character I felt that he and Emma had more romance scenes then her and Evan. Or maybe they just had more sex…*Shrugs* I guess I just would have loved more of her and Evan together as a couple.<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Most are lovable<br>Writing Style- Fair<br>Plot/Storyline- Infuriatingly frustrating, intense and dark<br>Steam Factor- Medium/Moderately steamy<br>Overall- Failed to hit the sweet spot :(<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5605942154540619659" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_424037794" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/424037794" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/424037794?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer424037794" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5250862200873194307"><b> 4 Still Breathing Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/2b0e2636-f44c-4626-a9a4-f1f330e9159e_zps2aaf153e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756036.jpg' alt=' photo 2b0e2636-f44c-4626-a9a4-f1f330e9159e_zps2aaf153e.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It’s been two years since Emma left Weslyn and went to Stanford for school. Two years since she’s left the past behind her, cutting off essentially everyone and everything except Sara and her roommates. She has been existing, but not living. Ever since she left her old life, ever since she left Evan, she’s been barley hanging on. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6eb86c92-1af7-495a-b5a9-41eec8acc356_zps8b318135.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756037.jpg' alt=' photo 6eb86c92-1af7-495a-b5a9-41eec8acc356_zps8b318135.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Emma is on a seriously self destructive path. Emma is out of control. Doing things she swore she would never do, acting out in ways I ne</span>
  <span id="freeText5250862200873194307" style="display:none"><b> 4 Still Breathing Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/2b0e2636-f44c-4626-a9a4-f1f330e9159e_zps2aaf153e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756036.jpg" alt=" photo 2b0e2636-f44c-4626-a9a4-f1f330e9159e_zps2aaf153e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s been two years since Emma left Weslyn and went to Stanford for school. Two years since she’s left the past behind her, cutting off essentially everyone and everything except Sara and her roommates. She has been existing, but not living. Ever since she left her old life, ever since she left Evan, she’s been barley hanging on. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6eb86c92-1af7-495a-b5a9-41eec8acc356_zps8b318135.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756037.jpg" alt=" photo 6eb86c92-1af7-495a-b5a9-41eec8acc356_zps8b318135.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Emma is on a seriously self destructive path. Emma is out of control. Doing things she swore she would never do, acting out in ways I never expected. She doesn’t let anyone in and pushes away everyone who tries to break through her barriers...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/c46adda6-161e-4f8e-a99a-2f5e58eee96b_zpsbc8101b4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756038.jpg" alt=" photo c46adda6-161e-4f8e-a99a-2f5e58eee96b_zpsbc8101b4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For the first time in two years, she meets someone who is persistent and won't give up on her. He understands as much as he can about Emma and takes things at her speed, gives her the space and distance she needs. His name is Cole... you heard that right, not Evan, but Cole. I wanted to hate Cole... I did. But I couldn’t. I really felt for the guy. Sara is out of the country and Emma is spiraling further out of control. A necessary trip back to Weslyn makes things even worse for her- she has to confront the man from her past... the man she left behind. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The only way to save you was to leave.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> This is were the book started to get even more intense. We have Emma who is acting out, Cole trying to be there for her, and Evan back into the picture. Talk about a mess! Emma doesn’t know what to do with herself, so she does what she does best. She tries to escape it, she runs.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/12060d01-5b8a-4527-a051-23edd106dd5d_zps680599e3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756039.jpg" alt=" photo 12060d01-5b8a-4527-a051-23edd106dd5d_zps680599e3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One thing I loved about this story is that we got dual pov’s the last half or so. As much as Emma drove me crazy at times, it was wonderful to get inside of Evan’s head. Evan is just amazing. He always has been, and he always will be. My heart broke for that boy over and over again. He finally finds out what was in that letter, and why Emma really left him... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <b><i>“I love him more than he will ever know. And because of that, I choose his happiness.” </i></b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <br>Evan is still hurt. What Emma put him through cut him deep. Regardless, Evan knows that he and Emma belong together, even if she doesn’t see it. Well, she see’s it, she just thinks she doesn’t deserve it. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m not supposed to live without you. And your not supposed to live without me. We’re in this life together. Without each other, we’re not really living.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Evan makes it his mission to show Emma that she deserves happiness, love, she deserves him. These two have a long road ahead of them full of healing, love, and forgiveness.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/4aef0ea2-563b-4684-a623-29c6db36227d_zpse8de8fdc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756040.jpg" alt=" photo 4aef0ea2-563b-4684-a623-29c6db36227d_zpse8de8fdc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>It pains me not to give this book 5 stars. This was one of the best series of 2012 for me. I have been waiting and waiting and waiting for this book to come out. There were parts of it I loved, but the first half just didn’t sit right with me. I understood why Emma was in so much pain and doing the things she was doing, I did. But the whole Cole situation... I dunno. And also things with Jonathan were strange to me... it seemed sort of anticlimactic. Evan saved the book for me. I love him. Just as much as I did in the first two books. I was happy with how it ended, but I desperately wanted more of an epilogue <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I wanted to see more of Emma and Evan later down the road <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The writing was fantastic, Emma’s journey was heartbreaking, frustrating and beautiful at the same time. The series is still a 5 star series for me. I still love it and I’m happy I read this one. Evan and Emma’s story is one that will stay with me forever!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/fab8bbdc-a73d-4d8d-ad74-8c2536eeffff_zps2932cd79.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392711i/756041.jpg" alt=" photo fab8bbdc-a73d-4d8d-ad74-8c2536eeffff_zps2932cd79.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_351674110" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/351674110" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/351674110?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351674110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14658225450769105332"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380381304i/738531._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='380' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>Disappointed-- 3 Stars for the writing not the story line</b><br/><br/>It feels like I’ve been waiting forever for this final installment of Rebecca Donovan’s Breathing Series. Like all fans, I wanted Emma and Evan to have their hea. The minute this book was released – the husband and kids were put on strict “do not disturb” warning. They have heard all about the books because I get all emotional when I talk about these characters. <br/><br/><i>Out of Breath</i> brings a reader two years after Emma left Weslyn for Stanford. </span>
  <span id="freeText14658225450769105332" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380381304i/738531._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Disappointed-- 3 Stars for the writing not the story line</b><br><br>It feels like I’ve been waiting forever for this final installment of Rebecca Donovan’s Breathing Series. Like all fans, I wanted Emma and Evan to have their hea. The minute this book was released – the husband and kids were put on strict “do not disturb” warning. They have heard all about the books because I get all emotional when I talk about these characters. <br><br><i>Out of Breath</i> brings a reader two years after Emma left Weslyn for Stanford. Emma is surrounded by a group of GREAT roommates and is in her sophomore year of college. Her relationship with Sara is still strong. They talk regularly while she is away in France and they see each over school breaks. <br><br>Emma has perfected being NUMB never letting thoughts of Carol, her cousins, Jonathan, her mother and of course Evan ever enter into her mind. On the outside she is excelling at school and sport but…the GUILT and SELF-LOATHING become overpowering and Emma searches to find adrenaline highs that can combat her pain. Feelings just keep piling up on Emma. <br><br><b>
  <i>”The black hole of emptiness that had protected me all of this time refused to shroud me in its shadows like I needed it to. I couldn’t shut everything off any more.”</i>
</b><br><br>Let’s be honest here... without Sara and her roommates I don’t think Emma would be functioning or even breathing. She’s like a fragile creature that everyone handles, protects and coddles. It's an around the clock --- "Emma Watch". <br><br>Emma meets a great guy named Cole although she pushes him away he does get under her skin. <br><br><b>
  <i>I needed him. I needed him in a way that probably wasn’t healthy for either of us. He was my fix. Even if he could never fix me.”</i>
</b><br><br>The story delivers one tragic blow after another on Emma. If you think that you are out of the woods on tragedy…think again! <br><br>I felt like I was stuck in a constant cycle of terrible news, Emma running till her feet fall off, Emma catatonic and depressed, Emma functioning…only to do it all over again.<br><br>I NEVER imagined that the author would have gone this route with this book. It was frustrating to read and absolutely heartbreaking to bear after all that a reader endured in the first two books.<br><br>Events bring Emma back in Weslyn where Evan and her paths meet up again. The reader will be ecstatic to learn that the book from this point on is in DUAL pov. <br><br><b>
  <i>”You’re supposed to hate me!” I couldn’t stop the tears from flowing or my body from shaking. “Why don’t you hate, Evan?!” My lip quivered.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>’Emma, I could never hate you. I’ve told you that before, and it’s still true.’ Her expectation that I could made me feel like she’d just punched a hole through my chest. ‘But I need closure, so I can move on.”</i>
</b><br><br>The cast of characters spend the majority of this book on the beautiful beaches of Santa Barbara for summer vacation. You see, Cole’s beach house happens to be down the road from Evan’s school chums. Emma agrees to give Evan two weeks to convince him to hate her and tell him the truth. <br><br>Slowly Emma lets Evan in and gives him the truths that he has so desperately needed. Please note that Jonathan does play a part in this story so readers beware. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I left Evan instead of letting him in. And I drove Jonathan away, fearful he’d gotten too close. Neither of them had a reason to trust me. No I was convinced I’d lost them both.”</i>
</b><br><br>Overall, the story was not what I expected or dreamed of but there is a conclusion and there is a hea. <br><br>The writing is very well done. I have tons of quotes highlighted throughout the book. Although, I didn’t care for the story line of tragedy and pain for the majority of the book, I think the emotional journey between the two characters was brilliantly done! <br><br>Now onto the epilogue…it was way too short! I believe readers <b>DESERVE</b> more of an epilogue for our pain and suffering. I’ll continue to hold my breath hoping that Rebecca Donovan gives readers more. She can think of it as our severance packages.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14658225450769105332" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_425427939" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/425427939" />
    <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite"><img alt="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368215503p2/3758447.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/425427939?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite">Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=extra-helping-of-drama">extra-helping-of-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=something-is-missing">something-is-missing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=where-did-the-ending-go">where-did-the-ending-go</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=traumatic-past">traumatic-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=what-the-f-happened">what-the-f-happened</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=skimed">skimed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=h-h-needs-a-2x4">h-h-needs-a-2x4</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=books-everyone-loved-but-me">books-everyone-loved-but-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer425427939" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8939594977103964995">2.5 stars<br/><br/><br/>***** Warning - rant, with some minor spoilers ********<br/><br/>What the hell was that? Seriously? Can somebody tell me how that was supposed to make be feel, because I'm pretty sure that it wasn't supposed to make me frustrated, annoyed, bored, and then frustrated again. <br/><br/>I didn't like Emma in this book at all. I get that she has been through a crap ton of horrible shit. I was very sympathetic to her in the previous two books, but in this one, I just wanted to scream at her to get the fuck over </span>
  <span id="freeText8939594977103964995" style="display:none">2.5 stars<br /><br /><br />***** Warning - rant, with some minor spoilers ********<br /><br />What the hell was that? Seriously? Can somebody tell me how that was supposed to make be feel, because I'm pretty sure that it wasn't supposed to make me frustrated, annoyed, bored, and then frustrated again. <br /><br />I didn't like Emma in this book at all. I get that she has been through a crap ton of horrible shit. I was very sympathetic to her in the previous two books, but in this one, I just wanted to scream at her to get the fuck over it. <br /><br />The book starts off a year and a half after Emma ran away from Evan and went to California. She has apparently been in emotional cold storage for all that time, and one party and a ton of booze brings her back to life. <br /><br />So, then we proceed with the excessive drinking portion of the book, where all of Emma's friends coddle her and make excuses/take the blame for her irresponsible behavior. It's not so much that I didn't get why she was self medicating, but it just seemed bizarre that she was ok for almost two years, and then *bam* alchi/adrenaline junkie Emma comes to life. <br /><br />It's during this period that we introduction our place holder Cole. Honestly, I don't get what Cole's role in the book was supposed to be. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ He never really gets close to Emma. He provides some mild angst when Evan comes back on the scene, but not too much. And then he crawls off with nary a whisper when Emma is ready to try again with Evan. So what was the point? What did he bring to the story? Was he just arm candy to keep us interested during Emma's self destruct phase? That's the best I can come up with. That said, I really liked Cole. I have no idea why he liked Emma, and I felt sincerely bad for the dude. He got the shaft big time, and he didn't deserve it. Also, the whole vibe of how they got together was SO similar to how she got together with Evan it was creepy. She's bitchy to him, he doesn't seem to care - hangs around even when she says she doesn't date, willing to take whatever she will give him etc. It just left me wondering what the heck was so special about Emma  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />After Evan comes back into Emma's life we enter the most frustrating part of the book. We can't just get down to things - sit down and have and honest heart to heart - no, we have to watch Emma wallow, interspersed with some parties, running, shopping, eating, surfing, camp outs and a whole bunch of crap that felt a while lot like filler to me. I was bored and frustrated. I hated Emma. She drove me nuts with her guilt and self flagellation. Every time you turn around she's breaking down, going semi-catatonic, doing something self-destructive. It was so OTT, I was exhausted. This was also the half of the book where we were treated to the dual Emma/Evan POVs. Normally, that would have been a treat, but we shifted back and forth so fast from one to the other, often in the middle of a scene, it gave me whiplash. <br /><br />Then, we finally get resolution - but do we get to bask in the fact that our couple is finally together again? Nope. After all that dragging things out, the end is about as wham, bam, thank you ma'am as I've read in a while. Zero satisfaction from the epilogue. <br /><br />This was one of those books I was so excited to finally read. I hate that I wish I hadn't bothered. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />********************<br />Ugh. I'm happy with where we ended up (excluding that epilogue) - but good lord, I wish we had gotten there ANY other way. Belch. <br /><br />I know this is going to be a minority opinion, big time. <br /><br />Full review to come.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8939594977103964995" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4827252267296494072"><b>ATTENTION, PEOPLE :</b><br/><br/><br/><i>Rebecca Donovan has just changed the cover for OUT OF BREATH:</i><br/><br/><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1367613888l/13638570.jpg' width='400' height='600' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>And, we also have a new teaser--------><br/><br/><br/><b>OUT OF BREATH Teaser:</b><br/><br/><br/><i>I closed my eyes, my chest tightening, knowing I wasn't ready.   <span id="freeText4827252267296494072" style="display:none"><b>ATTENTION, PEOPLE :</b><br><br><br><i>Rebecca Donovan has just changed the cover for OUT OF BREATH:</i><br><br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1367613888l/13638570.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>And, we also have a new teaser--------&gt;<br><br><br><b>OUT OF BREATH Teaser:</b><br><br><br><i>I closed my eyes, my chest tightening, knowing I wasn't ready.         rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer330524020" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6540505062064656782"><br/>4.5 ★'s<br/><br/>At the end of the last book, you know some horrible things had happened and that Emma took off to Stanford...and that's where I've been left hanging for the past year - imagining all sorts of scenarios that could be played out. None of them even came close to what happened in this book! Okay, okay...maybe the part where Evan shows up. <i>That</i> was definitely in ALL my scenarios! <br/><br/>This book, heck, <i>this series</i> is pretty depressing but there are some good moments too. It's really about a damaged </span>
  <span id="freeText6540505062064656782" style="display:none"><br>4.5 ★'s<br><br>At the end of the last book, you know some horrible things had happened and that Emma took off to Stanford...and that's where I've been left hanging for the past year - imagining all sorts of scenarios that could be played out. None of them even came close to what happened in this book! Okay, okay...maybe the part where Evan shows up. <i>That</i> was definitely in ALL my scenarios! <br><br>This book, heck, <i>this series</i> is pretty depressing but there are some good moments too. It's really about a damaged girl that finds hope in a boy and even though she tries to do the right thing, she ends up hurting him. Ultimately, she has to learn to forgive herself. <br><br>I could not believe how <i>broken</i> Emma was!! It was sooo hard to read about her thoughts and feelings. We all know this girl has been through hell and back and I can totally understand where she was coming from with wanting to NOT hurt Evan but TWO FREAKIN' YEARS?? WTH?? I was stunned, frustrated and confused but it only made me unable to stop reading the freakin' book! <br><br>And then enters Cole and I felt my heart breaking. Don't get me wrong, Cole is wonderful and probably a little of what Emma needed. I think without him, things might have been very different but still...Cole ≠ Evan...that is a fact. <br><br>Sooo...Evan. It was a little scary seeing these two broken people possibly try to work things out. After being through so much, could they trust each other enough to try to be together? As messed up as we know Emma was, I do have to say that I was taken back by how affected Evan was....and it is wrong to say that I was happy that even two years later, he is still so wrapped up in her? <br><br>It warmed my heart to read about the things Evan just knew would work for Emma...just goes to show that sometimes it takes people that really know you, to know what can help you. I loved how Evan and Sara were able to work together. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379795366i/604213._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All of Emma's roommates were wonderful especially Serena but they definitely are no replacement for Sara. I just love her even though she couldn't possibly be there for Emma 24/7. I hated seeing what she went through as well but I was happy with the way things worked out. <br><br>The drama! Crazy, crazy drama and right from the start with the first party and what Emma did (almost) - you just knew that things were going downhill...fast. And the dramas don't stop coming! <br><br>I think the only problem that I had with the book is with the way the different POVs are written. Emma's is plain text and Evan's is italic but several times I was so wrapped up in the story that it didn't register that the POV had changed and I had to start over so I could be in that person's head. <br><br>I was happy with the way things ended. We get a taste of things in the future with a short epilogue. But I also can't believe it's actually over and that's it. The end. :(<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/511080.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Favorite quotes: <br><br>♦ "So … you like the rain?" he enquired with a gleam in his eye.<br><br>"Yes, don’t you?" I asked, brushing my lips along his jaw, my pulse still thrumming. <br><br>"No," he replied with a chuckle. "I think I <i>love</i> the rain."<br><br>♥ <i>She had always connected with that tree too, making it the perfect location for the swing I’d made for her. <br><br>The swing that I’d hoped would keep her coming back here. Back to me.</i><br><br>♥ <i> "Pink’s my chocolate," she whispered.</i><br><br>♥ "You don’t have to <i>let me</i>, Emma. I already do. You just have to love me back. With everything you have. And that’s all I need. I need <i>you. All</i> of you."<br><br>♥ "I’m not supposed to live without you. And you’re not supposed to live without me. We’re in this life together. Without each other, we’re not really living."<br><br>♥ I just had to remember, there was always a choice. And I chose to live. I chose to love. I chose to breathe.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/596850.gif" width="400" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6540505062064656782" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
